shell2 defines the envelope of thescooter1 and thevehicle1 is frameless.Suspensions42, 82 of at least twowheels40, 80 are connected to theplastic shell2. Theplastic shell2 of thevehicle1 forms a structural portion of thevehicle1, as opposed to a conventional scooter in which the plastic shell forms only an aesthetic outer body supported by an inner structural frame. Therefore, the conventional metal inner frame for supporting thewheel suspensions42 and 82 can be omitted. Placing all load-bearing structural materials at the outermost cross-sectional points of the structural portion formed by theplastic shell2 can increase stiffness and strength by up to four orders of magnitude. This allows for a reduction in the total weight of thevehicle1 and a significant increase in internal space while simultaneously increasing strength and rigidity. The weight reduction provides faster acceleration and wider range on the same drivetrain, thereby reducing costs and increasing the resource efficiency ofvehicle1. Due to the increased internal space, there is room for up to 6xlarger battery pack116 and up to 6x larger storage space. Since less material is used in thelighter vehicle1, the cost of thevehicle1 can be further reduced.æ§è½ãã¦ã¼ã¶ã®ãã¼ãºã«é©åãããããã®æè»æ§ãã¦ã¼ã¶ã«æä¾ããããã«ãããããªã¼ããã¯ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãå¥½ã¾ããã¯ãã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«å¼ããããªã¼ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ï¼ï¼ï¼å³ï¼ï¼ãåãããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿æ¬ä½ã¯ãã°ãã°åçåãããå°è±¡ãä¸ããããã«æ¹¾æ²ãã¦ããã®ã§ãååãªå®¹éã®åä¸ã®å¤§ããªããããªã¼ã¯ãå¤§ããã¦é·æ¹å½¢ã§ãããã¨ãå¤ããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿æ¬ä½ã®åé¨ã«åå®¹ããã®ãé£ãããè¤æ°ã®ããå°ããªã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ï¼ï¼ãè¨­ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦ãåãã®çµã¿åããããããããªã¼ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã¯ãå ´åã«ãã£ã¦ã¯ããã¤ãã®å¥åã®å ´æã§ããããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿æ¬ä½ã®åé¨è¼ªé­ã«åå®¹ããã®ãããå®¹æã«ãªããããããªã¼ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ï¼ã®ãããã¬ã¹ãï¼ï¼ã®ä¸ã«éç½®ãããåº§å¸­ï¼ï¼ãæã¡ä¸ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦ã¢ã¯ã»ã¹ãããã¨ããåãå¤ããã¨ãäº¤æãããã¨ãã§ãããIn order to provide the user with the flexibility to adapt the performance to the user's needs, thebattery pack116 preferably comprises a modular battery module 118 (FIG. 2). A single large battery of sufficient capacity is often large and rectangular and difficult to fit inside the scooter body, as the scooter body is often curved to give a streamlined impression. By providing multiplesmaller modules118, the individual combined battery modules are more easily accommodated in the internal contours of the scooter body, even in some separate locations. Thebattery116 is located under thefootrest22 of thescooter1 and can be accessed, removed or replaced by lifting theseat24.ãã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã«é©ããææã¯ãä¾ãã°ãç­ç´ ãã¬ã©ã¹ãã¢ã©ããããã¤ãã¼ãï¼ç»é²åæ¨ï¼ãããã³ç±ç¡¬åæ§ã¾ãã¯ç±å¯å¡æ§ãããªãã¯ã¹ä¸­ã®ä»ã®ç¹ç¶­ãªã©ã®ç¹ç¶­å¼·åããªãã§ãããSuitable materials for theplastic shell2 are fiber reinforced polymers such as, for example, carbon, glass, aramid, DyneemaÂ®, and other fibers in thermosetting or thermoplastic matrices.ã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ï¼ã®ãã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã¯ãå¾è¼ªï¼ï¼ãåå®¹ããããã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®è»è¼ªã±ã¼ã·ã³ã°ï¼ï¼ã¨ãåè¼ªï¼ï¼ãåå®¹ããããã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®è»è¼ªã±ã¼ã·ã³ã°ï¼ï¼ã¨ãåãããTheplastic shell2 of thescooter1 includes afirst wheel casing18 for accommodating therear wheels40 and a second wheel casing 20 for accommodating thefront wheels80.å¥½ã¾ããã¯ãè»è¼ªï¼ï¼ãï¼ï¼ã®å°ãªãã¨ãï¼ã¤ã¯ãã·ã§ãã¯ã¢ãã½ã¼ãï¼ï¼ãï¼ï¼ãåãããå³ç¤ºã®å®æ½å½¢æã§ã¯ãå¾è¼ªï¼ï¼ã«ã·ã§ãã¯ã¢ãã½ã¼ãï¼ï¼ãè¨­ããããåè¼ªï¼ï¼ã«ã·ã§ãã¯ã¢ãã½ã¼ãï¼ï¼ãè¨­ãããããã·ã§ãã¯ã¢ãã½ã¼ãï¼ï¼ãï¼ï¼ãä½¿ç¨ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦ãåè¨è»ä¸¡ï¼ã®ä½¿ç¨ä¸­ã«è»è¼ªãµã¹ãã³ã·ã§ã³ï¼ï¼ãï¼ï¼ãããã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã«ä¼éããããã¼ã¯åãæ¸å°ããããããã£ã¦ããã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ãåãããã¼ã¯è·éã¯æ¸å°ãããPreferably, at least one of thewheels40, 80 comprisesshock absorbers44, 84. of at least one drivenwheel40 includes aswing arm62 together with an integrated motor housing 64 (FIGS. 7-9). Themotor housing64 is configured to accommodate theelectric motor114. Integrating themotor housing64 with theswing arm62 into a single component has several advantages. First, the number of components is reduced, which simplifies the assembly of thevehicle1. Second, the total heat capacity of the material of therear swing arm62 can now function as a heat sink for themotor114, creating a substantially larger heat sink and a larger heat sink surface. This reduces the need to actively cool themotor114. Third, the distance between themotor114 and thepulley72 is constant, providing a reliable drive arrangement. In addition, the placement of thepivot axis66 of therear swingarm62 significantly reduces the unsprung weight by balancing the weight of themotor114 with the weight of the rear of the swingarm 62 (along with the wheels), thereby springing and damping. pack116 is modular so that increasing or decreasing the number ofmodules118 in thebattery pack116 does not affect the normal voltage of the battery pack and no additional electronics or controls are needed to ensure safe operation. Can be. This characteristic of constant normal voltage is highly desirable as the power consuming component is identified according to a particular voltage and optimally performed at that particular voltage. Connecting thebattery modules118 in series would multiply the voltage by the number ofbattery modules118, as opposed to connecting thebattery modules118 in parallel. The latter provides a battery voltage spectrum that is more than sufficient for the optimum dimensions of the vehicle's power consuming device. However, connecting modules in parallel without expensive power management electronics can result in inrush currents betweenbattery modules118 and (sudden) differences in module voltage caused by cell malfunction or differences in cell internal resistance. Dangerous due to other unwanted effects that may occur. Therefore, thebattery pack116 connects thecell clusters1 to X of the first battery module to Y, respectively (for example, the first cell cluster of thefirst battery module118 is the first cell cluster of thesecond battery module118. Thesecond battery module118 is connected to the first cell cluster of thethird battery module118, and so on, to the Yth battery module 118). It can be equipped with abattery module118 that is interconnected using. X represents the number of cell clusters perbattery module118, and Y is the total number ofbattery modules118. As a result, all independent voltage levels of the connected battery modules 118 (which together form the battery pack 116) are interconnected, requiring additional power management electronics per module to ensure safe operation. Does not generate a constant normal voltage. To increase the safety level of thebattery pack116, all individual cells are sized by an aluminum interconnect (between the cell and the busbar of the cell cluster) that is sized to weld if the current exceeds a certain level. Double welded. This configuration of thebattery pack116 allows the user to upgrade or downgrade the number ofbattery modules118 in thescooter1 and effectively increase or decrease the range as needed (eg, daily commute distance). Due to changes in). Further, if one of thebattery modules118 fails, it is possible to replace only thedefective battery module188.ã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼ã¯ãé§åãã«ãï¼ï¼ããã³ãã¼ãªï¼ï¼ãä»ãã¦é§åãããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ï¼ã®å¾è¼ªï¼ï¼ãæ¯æãããã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼ã«ã¯ãä¸ä½åãã«ãã¬ã¼ãï¼ï¼ãè¨­ãããããä¸ä½åãã«ãã¬ã¼ãï¼ï¼ã¯ãéè»¢èã®è¶³ãæããã«ãããä¿è­·ããåå¥ã®ä¿è­·è£ç½®ã®å¿è¦æ§ãæé¤ãããTheswing arm62 supports therear wheel40 of thescooter1 driven via thedrive belt70 and thepulley72. engineering design structure of thebase plate52 has been optimized to allow for the most ideal and shortest possible force paths within this configuration. Thespring46 and theshock absorber44 are connected to thebase plate52 by apivot47. The distance between thepivot point47 of onespring46 and theshock absorber44 and thepivot axis66 of the otherrear swing arm62 is such that therear spring46 is placed parallel to theswing arm62 and the front spring mounting point is electrically connected. Optimized by placing as close as possible to the sides of themotor114 to provide the shortest load path and the most compact assembly. In order to achieve the shortest possible load path and compact assembly, therear spring46 is swivelly located at the top of theswingarm62 and requires the required spring force and spring force of theswingarm62,base plate52 andplastic shell2. Form an arm long enough to reduce the peak load. This setting creates additional usable space in thebuddy space25 under theseat24. By forming a short load path, it is possible to integrate thepivot point47 of onespring46 andshock absorber44 with thepivot point66 of the otherrear swing arm62, resulting in significantly more accurate manufacturing tolerances and Allows for asingle base plate52 that is compatible, preferably made of aluminum. In addition to further reducing the number of parts, this reduces the manufacturing tolerances required for theplastic shell2 and reduces manufacturing costs as it only requires a single manufacturing step to obtain the desired manufacturing tolerances. ..å ãã¦ããã¼ã¹ãã¬ã¼ãï¼ï¼ã®ä¸è¿°ã®å·¥å­¦çè¨­è¨æ§é ã¯ãåæ§ããã³å¼·åº¦ãé«ããã°ã­ï¼ï¼ã®åããã¼ã¹ãã¬ã¼ãï¼ï¼ã®æ¢å­ã®å¹¾ä½å­¦çå½¢ç¶ã«æ°´å¹³æ¹åã«è·éä¼éãããã¨ãå¯è½ã«ãããã®åãå¸åããã®ã«å¿è¦ãªè¿½å ã®ææã®éãæ¸ãããã¨ãã§ãããIn addition, the above-mentioned engineering design structure of thebase plate52 increases rigidity and strength, allowing the force of thespring44 to be horizontally transferred to the existing geometry of thebase plate52 and absorb this force. The metal is strong, has excellent thermal conductivity properties, and allows heat transfer to the environment from themotor housing64 and / or thebase plate52. Therefore, themotor housing64 and / or thebase plate52 can function as a heat sink. This heat sink functions as both a thermal mass and a heat dissipation surface. This allows heat to be transferred to the environment efficiently and passively, significantly reducing the need for active cooling and eliminating components that require complex maintenance.ããå¥½ã¾ããã¯ãã¢ã¼ã¿ãã¦ã¸ã³ã°ï¼ï¼ã¨ãã¼ã¹ãã¬ã¼ãã®ä¸¡æ¹ã¯ãéå±è£½ã§ãããã¢ã¼ã¿ï¼ï¼ï¼ãã¢ã¼ã¿ãã¦ã¸ã³ã°ï¼ï¼ã«åå®¹ãããªã¢ã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼å¨ä½ã¯ãé»æ°ã¢ã¼ã¿ï¼ï¼ï¼ã«ãã£ã¦çºçãããç±ã®ããã®ãã¼ãã·ã³ã¯ã¨ãã¦æ©è½ããããã®å¾ãç±ã¯ããªã¢ã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼ã®å¨è¾ºã®ç©ºæ°æµã«æ¾æ£ããããMore preferably, both themotor housing64 and the base plate are made of metal. Thefins60 form a larger heat transfer surface for dissipating heat to the air and are in direct thermal contact with one or more exothermicelectronic components120 that are thermally mounted on the top of thebase plate52. Such anelectronic component120 may include one or more of a battery management system, a motor controller, a charger, a (DC / DC) converter and an electronic control unit (ECU) 120. The two funnel-shapedportions10, 16 are aligned and thehead tube98 extends between both funnel-shapedportions10, 16. Due to the distance between the two funnel-shapedportions10, 16, thehead tube98 is firmly supported by theplastic shell2, so that running forces such as bumps and braking forces are facilitated by thewheel suspension82 of thefront wheels80. The resulting upward force is transmitted to thefork108 and then to theshock absorber84, thereby reducing and dampening the peak load. Theshock absorber84 then transfers the resulting residual damping force to thehead tube98. Through thebearing100, this force is then guided through theplastic shell2 to the support surface 88 forming the first connector 86. The plate 102 forms the support surface 88 and abuts on the firstfront contact surface6 of theplastic shell2. The wall of theplastic shell2 of the lower funnel-shapedportion10 is predominantly loaded by a tensile force directed substantially along the wall.åè¼ªï¼ï¼ã«ããå¶åä¸­ããã¬ã¼ã­ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãåè¼ªï¼ï¼ãä»ãã¦è»ä¸¡ï¼ã®éåã¨ãã«ã®ã¼ãå¸åãããããã«ãããè»ä¸¡ã®è³ªéã«ãã£ã¦å¼ãèµ·ããããåè¼ªï¼ï¼ãåããæ¸éåãçããããã®çµæãï¼ã¤ã®ç®æãããªãã¡ç¬¬ï¼ã®åæ¹å½æ¥é¢ï¼ããã³ç¬¬ï¼ã®åæ¹å½æ¥é¢ï¼ã§ãã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã«åãä¼éããããããã«ãããã·ã§ã«å¨ä½ã«ä»¥ä¸ã®åãåéããããDuring braking by thefront wheels80, the braking system absorbs the kinetic energy of thevehicle1 through thefront wheels80. This causes the deceleration force that thefront wheels80 receive, which is caused by the mass of the vehicle. As a result, the force is transmitted to theplastic shell2 at two points, that is, the firstfront contact surface6 and the secondfront contact surface8. Therefore, thefront panel12 and the leg shield 14 are predominantly loaded in the preferred direction, i.e., on the wall of the plastic shell 2 (rather than laterally). The deceleration also induces rear-to-front weight transfer, providing greater vertical force on thefront wheels80. shown in FIGS. 11 and 12,vehicle1 comprises adisplay34 having a user interface such as an operating system or application. The steering 28 of thescooter1 comprises one or more control interfaces 32. In the figure, theleft control interface32L and theright control interface32R are shown. Thecontrol interface32 is designed to securely control the entire operating system and all functions required to control one or more applications running on the operating system and displayed on thedisplay34. Potentially, the control interface may be used additionally or alternatively to control other personal devices connected, for example via Bluetooth. The one ormore control interfaces32 are arranged so that the driver does not have to hold thesteering28 by himself and the control can be used blindly. Detailed views of theleft control interface32L and theright control interface32R are shown in FIGS. 13A and 13B, respectively. FIG. 14 shows a side view of theleft control interface32L of FIG. 13A, but it should be noted that the right control interface has a similar configuration. The structural rubber of thecontrol interface32 shown in the perspective view of FIG. 15 allows the user to clearly identify the current position of the thumb via the touch, and further controls thecontrol buttons32L-1 to 32L-8 and 32R-1 to. It is sized and configured to allow blind navigation between 32R-8. This is achieved by the dome-shaped structure as seen in the side view of FIG. The wall thickness of thebuttons32L-1 to 32L-8 and 32R-1 to 32R-8 provides good press control and recognition, even with gloved hands, and in rain and various operating conditions. It is configured to be susceptible to sufficient pressure to enable it. Thebutton interface32L on the left side of thesteering28 has eight buttons, five of which have the following standard scooter functions: leftwinker32L-1, right winker 32L3, high /low beam selection32L-6, alarm.Light32L-7, horn 32L-8.Buttons32L-22, 32L-4 and 32L-5 are used for music / video volume control and music / video playback, and both of thescooter1's built-in speakers 36 (preferably the touch screen display 34). It has the ability to control the volume of the left speaker 36L and / or the right speaker 36R) next to it and / or the volume of a connected personal device such as a smartphone. Preferably, the connection is a wireless connection, for example via Bluetooth. Preferably, the user can control the playback of any audio / video stream on both thetouch screen34 and the connected personal device.Button32L-2 is used for volume up,button32L-4 is used for volume down,button32L-5 is used for play, pause and next and previous songs. The latter two are done by pressing twice or three times, control interface32R on the right side of the steering 28 also has eight buttons in a similar layout, but preferably has significantly different functions. Theright buttons32R-1 to 32R-8 are all specially configured to control the operating system and all applications that can be performed while driving. As mentioned above, other personal devices can also be controlled using abutton32, for example a device connected via Bluetooth, or any other connection such as an MP3 player or any alternative device. .. Preferably, thebuttons32R-1 to 32R-4 are omnidirectional controls for navigating different applications and their respective focusable user interface (UI) elements.Button32R-1 is on the left, 32R-2 is on the top, 32R-3 is on the right, and 32R-4 is on the bottom. Thesenavigation buttons32R-1 to 32R-4 may be replaced by a single rotary button that may resemble a short joystick, such as that normally found in some embodiments of laptop computer keyboards.Button32R-5 is used to click on a UI element selected by single click or open search when no element is selected. shown in FIG. 2, thescooter1 includes aseat24. Asensor26, such as a pressure sensor, is located below theseat24. Thesensor26 is configured to detect the presence of the driver in theseat24. Thesensor26 is connected to the control unit of thevehicle1, for example, theelectronic component120. Thecontrol component120 may be a motor controller configured to allow theelectric motor114 to drive thevehicle1 only when the user is sitting in the seat. Thesensor26 further controls thecontrol unit120 or 171 with braking characteristics such as throttle response, motor torque, motor speed, speed, maximum current drawn from the energy storage system, distribution, maximum braking power, anti-blocking system parameters or braking, vehicle. Loads (driver, passenger) to allow the characteristics of thescooter1 to be adapted, such as dynamics, adjustments to the scooter's load weight (changes) such as suspension parameters (rigidity, damping coefficient). , And / or the weight of the cargo) can be recorded. For example, heavier weight can increase rigidity, increase damping, and adjust the throttle response so that it is not steep, preventing passengers from falling off the scooter, but both the driver and the passenger. Motor power can be increased for such and / or other scooter characteristics when the load on the scooter is low to provide sufficient power to carry. As a result of pairing, the public key of the key fob is stored in the secure key storage in the vehicle or with equivalent security, and the cryptographically secure checksum of the public key list of the insecure storage is the insecure storage. Stored in secure storage to avoid tampering, both methods are called secure key storage. This secure key storage puts the vehicle in a software state that allows such operation by a user or by a command that has been verified to come from a previously authorized source programmed into the vehicle at the time of manufacture. Protected from modification, copying and other unauthorized operations, except where it is. The first method requires the key fob to be within range of the vehicle. The vehicle's central controller is placed in a special software state to accept new keys. Then press the key fob button. The key fob sends a message to the vehicle and responds with a special challenge message to the key fob that the vehicle needs to send the public key. The key fob responds to this challenge message by sending the public key. The vehicle stores this public key in secure key storage.2. 2. In the second method, the key fob public key is added to the list of key fob public keys allowed by programming commands from a remote device, eg, using the internet or a private back office connection, if available. To. The programming command includes a public key and an encrypted signature that ensures that the programming command was generated by a previously authorized source.è»ä¸¡ã®ã»ã­ã¥ãªãã£ã¯ãã­ã¼ãã©ãå¬ééµã®ãªã¹ããè¨±å¯ããã¦ããªãæä½ã¾ãã¯ä¿®æ­£ããä¿è­·ããè½åã«ä¾å­ãããããéµãã­ã°ã©ãã³ã°ã³ãã³ããçæãããã¨ãè¨±å¯ãããªããã°ãªããªãã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãããããã§ãããã¨ã«çæãããããIt normal operation, the key fob functions as follows. The key fob must be within range of the vehicle for it to work. When a key fob button is pressed, the key fob broadcasts a message that contains the code of the pressed button (each button in the key fob has a unique code). Security can also be implemented by including an encrypted signature based on the key fob's private key already included in this message, or an alternative or in addition to a challenge-response mechanism that works as follows: Also available: When the vehicle receives this message, it responds by broadcasting a challenge message. Upon receiving this message, the key fob performs a cryptographically secure calculation based on the challenge message sent by the vehicle as well as the private key, broadcasts the calculation result and re-includes the button code. The vehicle receives this message and encrypts it using the public key received from the key fob (stored in the vehicle using one of the methods described below) to verify the identity of the key fob. Run the algorithm. The encryption feature used in both methods ensures that the key fob's ID is verified when the message verification is successful, and conversely the message verification fails when a device other than the real key fob is used. Must. A preferred part of this method is that the key fob must respond to the challenge transmitted by the vehicle, and the challenge changes each time to prevent a replay attack. Different encryption algorithms and key types can be used to achieve the same result. In future systems, the vehicle will also be able to broadcast the challenge message without the key fob having to send the message first, which does not affect the effectiveness of the other steps of the method described above.ããã§æ³¨ç®ãããã®ã¯ãåè¿°ã®ã¢ãã­ã¼ãã¯ãä¸­ç¶æ»æã«å¯¾ãããããªãã»ã­ã¥ãªãã£ãå¿è¦ã¨ããå¯è½æ§ããããã¨ã§ãããããã¯ããã¼ãã¯ã¤ã¤ã¼ãã¾ãã¯ã¢ã¤ã³ã³ãã¿ã³ãã¦ã¼ã¶ã«ãã£ã¦æ¼ãããå¿è¦ããããã¨ãè¦æ±ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦è»½æ¸ããå¾ããããã¿ã³ãæ¼ãå¿è¦ããªãååã·ã¹ãã ãä½¿ç¨ããå ´åãã¡ãã»ã¼ã¸ã®å°çã«é¢ãã¦æéå¶éãèª²ãå¿è¦ãããããããããããã¯ããç§ã®ãªã¼ãã§ãããå½æ¥­èã¯ããã®ãããªç¹å¾´ãã©ã®ããã«å®è£ãããã«ã¤ãã¦èºèºããªãã§ããããIt is worth noting here that the aforementioned approach may require additional security against man-in-the-middle attacks. This can be mitigated by requiring that the hardwired or icon button need to be pressed by the user, but if you use a passive system that does not require the button to be pressed, you need to impose a time limit on the arrival of the message. There may be, it is on the order of nanoseconds. An internet connection can be achieved by including a cellular communication device in the vehicle, or by using a link to the cellular communication of the user's mobile device, a WiFi connection (which is increasingly appearing in public places), and the like. Such cellular communication devices can be connected to one or several controllers in the vehicle. If only one controller is connected to the cellular communication device, communication for the other controllers needs to be done via the available interconnect in the vehicle or in the user's mobile device. This can be done by including the software module in the controller connected to the cellular communication device performing this gateway function. And since the user interface controller does not have the private key used to sign the control message, any modification of the control message through the user interface controller will result in an invalid signature, so such a message will be delivered by the central controller. It will be destroyed. Therefore, any security breach with respect to the user interface controller should not allow the user interface controller to send control messages. Any control message that can be issued by the user interface controller must most preferably be signed with a private key that is unique to the user interface controller. The user interface controller software may be responsible for protecting access to this private key.æ»æãæ¤åºãã¦æ»æããä¿è­·ããããã«ãããã¤ã¹ã¯ãå¤±æããç½²åæ¤è¨¼ã®æ°ãè¿½è·¡ãããããç£è¦ãã¼ã¿ã«å«ãããã¨ãã§ããããã®ãããªå¤±æããç½²åæ¤è¨¼ã®æ°ã¯ãããã¤ã¹ãæ»æããè©¦ã¿ããã³ããã¤ã¹ã¸ã®ä¸æ­£ãªã¢ã¯ã»ã¹ã®è©¦ã¿ã®å¯è½æ§ãç¤ºãå¾ããTo detect and protect against attacks, the device can track the number of failed signature verifications and include this in the monitoring data. In this way, for all senders, it is possible to generate an encrypted secret that is specific to the connection between the controller and the sender, or that can be dedicated to the connection. Secrets may be established and exchanged using appropriate methods for exchanging secrets over unencrypted channels, such as the Diffie-Hellman key exchange protocol. In that case, the secret can be stored in secure key storage and cannot be retrieved from the device. On the sender side, all messages are encrypted with a shared secret and propagated over the cellular network. On the recipient side, the message is decrypted with a shared secret and then further Isolation User Interface In an embodiment of the disclosure in which the controller uses a cellular network connection to provide internet access to various applications, it monitors and controls the messages exchanged between the central controller and the secure server. Can act as a gateway for At some point, this traffic may need to be isolated. In embodiments according to the present disclosure, this creates at least two connections to the cellular network, that is, at least one connection having public internet access, and at least one connection having a private and secure connection to a secure server. Can be done by This separation can be implemented in cellular networks by using different access point names (APNs) for each. The controller can create one network device for each connection. Network devices can have different IP ranges. Private network traffic can have a private IP range. The network traffic of the application running on the gateway controller may be routed by the operating system depending on the IP address used when opening the network connection.ã»ã«ã©ãããã¯ã¼ã¯ã®ããã¯ã¨ã³ãå´ã§ã¯ããã¹ã¦ã®ãã©ã¤ãã¼ãï¼¡ï¼°ï¼®ãã©ãã£ãã¯ã¯ãå®å¨ãªãµã¼ãã«éä¿¡ãããã¨ãã§ãããOn the addition to the above disclosure, the system for controlling and monitoring the vehicle is, for example, a central controller connected to thebasic display176 and a user connected to thedisplay174, for example for more entertainment related applications. It should be noted that an interface controller, anicon display176 showing legally required driving-related information and safety information, a touch-enableddisplay174, and a large number ofbuttons32 for basic input can be provided. More specifically, the central controller may be connected to the user interface controller by a dedicated communication bus, the central controller may be connected to the icon display by a dedicated communication bus, and the central controller may be buttoned by a dedicated communication bus. It may be connected to a part of. In addition, the central controller may be connected to all other electrical systems except buttons, user interface controllers and icon displays by one or several communication buses, the user interface controller for dedicated video bus and touch control. The dedicated bus may be connected to the touch-enabled display, and the user interface controller may be connected to a part of the button by the dedicated communication bus. user can unlock the vehicle without the need for a physical key. The physical locks such as the cable lock of the base plate, the steering lock and drive train lock of theswing arm62 and the luggage space lock can be controlled by said application of an external electronic device such as a telephone or key fob (as described above). .. The vehicle also comprises one or more luggage spaces that can be opened remotely. If the user rents a vehicle from the owner of the vehicle and requires, for example, a helmet, the user can use the electronic device or the application of the key fob, for example, when the user is near the vehicle to obtain a physical key. You can open the luggage space without the need for. Such proximity can be determined by comparing position signals from both the user and the vehicle. Position signals can be estimated, for example, from GPS signals from said vehicles, Bluetooth and / or cellular connections, or by other means. The luggage space can be opened, for example, by unlocking it with an electromechanical actuator. The vehicle may be further locked by a virtual lock. This virtual lock can be unlocked in multiple ways. The virtual lock can be unlocked by a physical key fob that wirelessly communicates with the vehicle, for example by NFC technology. Another method for releasing the virtual lock is by using an electronic device such as a telephone that wirelessly communicates with the vehicle, for example via Bluetooth or NFC technology. Such wireless communication requires that the device be enabled by the application to unlock a particular vehicle. Another method is by unlocking the vehicle via an internet connection. Another method of unlocking the vehicle may be by entering a particular code, password, or pattern into the vehicle's display or the user's personal electronic portable device. The other means of unlocking the vehicle may be, but is not limited to, a fingerprint or an iris scanner. Vehicle1 under thefootrest22 for the purpose of supplying electrical energy to the drive system as well as all other electrical systems (eg lights, sensors, central (vehicle) controllers, controllers (s), etc.). It has an arrangedbattery116. Thebattery116 has a modular design structure and comprisesseveral battery modules118, meaning that the capacity can be increased or decreased by adding or removingmodules118 respectively. Thebattery118 consists of at least one module and, if possible, more modules. Modules can be electrically connected in parallel. The parallel connection of thebattery modules118 allows the battery assembly to be distributed inside the shell or body of the scooter, eg, in the space under thefootrest22, allowing it to supply sufficient power (current), while providing sufficient power (current). The combined battery is always rated at the same maximum and minimum voltage regardless of the number of modules. This has the advantage that expensive power electronics such as additional BMS slaves can be omitted. In addition, all power electronics can be rated at the same voltage level, reducing costs. The maximum current output from the battery increases as the number of modules increases. However, the cost of high current rated fuses and wires is much lower than the cost of high voltage rated power electronics.ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãï¼ã¤ã¾ãã¯è¤æ°ã®ããããªã¼ã»ã«ãããªãå¾ãããããã®ã»ã«ã¯ãææã®é»å§ããã³å®¹éåºåã«éããããã«ãä¸¦åãããã¯ç´åã¾ãã¯ãã®ä¸¡æ¹ã«æ¥ç¶ãããã¨ãã§ãããã»ã«ã®ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ã¯ãé»å§ãä¸ããã«ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã®å®¹éãå¢ããããã«ä¸¦åã«æ¥ç¶ãããã»ã«ã§ãããã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ã¯ãï¼ã¤ä»¥ä¸ã®ã»ã«ãããªãå¾ããè¤æ°ã®ã»ã«ã¾ãã¯ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ãä½¿ç¨ãã¦ãããããç´åã«æ¥ç¶ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã®é»å§åºåãå¢å ããããã¨ãã§ãããè¤æ°ã®ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã®é»å§ã¬ãã«ã®å·®ã«ãã£ã¦å¼ãèµ·ããããçªå¥é»æµãé²æ­¢ããããã«ãï¼¢ï¼­ï¼³ãªã©ã¯ãè¤æ°ã®ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã«ãããã»ã«ã¾ãã¯ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ã®é»å§ãç£è¦ããã³å¹³è¡¡åãããã¨ãã§ãããããã¯ãç¹å®ã®ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ã®ããããã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ãã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ï¼ï½ã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ã«é»æ°çã«ä¸¦åã«æ¥ç¶ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦è¡ããããããã§ãï½ã¯ãï¼ã¨ããããªã¼ãåããå­å¨ããã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã®ç·æ°ï¼ï¼ã¨ã®éã§ãããä¾ãã°ãã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ï¼ã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ã¯ããã¹ã¦ã®ä»ã®ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã®ãã¹ã¦ã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ããã³ï¼¢ï¼­ï¼³ã«æ¥ç¶ããã¦ããããå³ï¼ï¼ã¯ãããããï¼ã¤ã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ãæããï¼ã¤ã®ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ãããã³ãããã®æ¥ç¶ã®ä¾ç¤ºçãªæ¦ç¥å³ãç¤ºããé»æ°çæ¥ç¶ã¯ãéãªã©ã®ä»»æã®å°é»ææãä»ãã¦ç¢ºç«ããããããã¯ããã¹ãã¼ãã¯ã¤ã¤ãæº¶æ¥ãªã©ã®å½¢æã§ããå¾ããé»æ°çæ¥ç¶ã¯ããããªãææã¾ãã¯é¨åãè¿½å ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦å®ç¾ããã¦ãããããããã¯è¨­è¨ã«ãã£ã¦ã¢ã¸ã¥ã¼ã«ã«æ¢ã«å­å¨ãã¦ããããããã«ãããä¸è¿°ã®ããã«ãã¹ã¦ã®ã»ã«ã¯ã©ã¹ã¿ãäºãã may consist of one or more battery cells. These cells can be connected in parallel, in series, or both to reach the desired voltage and capacitive output. A cluster of cells are cells that are connected in parallel to increase the capacity of the module without increasing the voltage. A cluster can consist of two or more cells. Multiple cells or clusters can be used to increase the voltage output of the module by connecting them in series. To prevent inrush currents caused by differences in voltage levels between multiple modules, BMS and the like can monitor and balance the voltage of cells or cell clusters across multiple modules. This is done by electrically connecting each cell cluster of aparticular module1 to the cell cluster ofmodule1 + n in parallel. Here, n is between 0 and the total number of existing modules -1 with batteries. For example, the third cell cluster ofmodule1 may be connected to all third cell clusters and BMS of all other modules. FIG. 22 shows an exemplary schematic of three modules, each with three cell clusters, and their connections. Electrical connections are established via any conductive material such as copper. This can be in the form of busbars, wires, welds and the like. Electrical connections may be realized by adding additional materials or components, or may already be present in the module by design. This allows the modules to be easily connected to each other without the need for additional assembly steps to connect all the cell clusters to each other as described above. Finally, the two poles (plus and minus) of the module are connected to each other in parallel with each other as described above. This can be done by adding additional parts such as busbars or wires, or by modular design. For example, the first module can be mechanically connected to the second module while simultaneously connecting all the required electrical connections. Mechanical connections may be made, for example, by bolting, clicking and / or tightening mechanisms.ããããªã¼ãçµã¿ç«ã¦ãããè»ä¸¡ã«åãä»ãããã¨ãã§ãããããããªã¼ãããã¦åããã¨ãé²æ­¢ããããã«ãããããªã¼ã¯åãä»ããå¾ãåºå®å·ãªã©ã®çµã¿ç«ã¦æ¸ã¿ã®ç¹å¾´ã«ãã£ã¦å®ä½ç½®ã«åºå®ãããããããã®åºå®å·ã¯ããã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã«æ©æ¢°çã«æ¥ç¶ãããã¨ãã§ãããOnce the battery is assembled, it can be attached to the vehicle. To prevent the battery from slipping and moving, the battery is installed and then fixed in place by pre-assembled features such as fixtures. These fixtures can be mechanically connected to theplastic shell2.ãã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã¸ã®ããããªã¼ã®çµç«ã¦ã¯ãæ¬¡ã®ããã«ãã¦éæãããã¨ãã§ãããããããªã¼ã¯ãã·ã¼ãã®ä¸ã®éå£é¨ãéã£ã¦è»ä¸¡ã®åé¨ã¹ãã¼ã¹ã«å¥ããããå¾ã®çµç«ã¹ãããã«ããã¦ãããã£ã¹ãã¼ã¹ãåãä»ãããããããããªã¼ã¯ãããããªã¼ã®çµç«ã¦ã®ããã«å©ç¨å¯è½ãªæãåæ¹ã®å¯è½ãªä½ç½®ã«åå®¹ãããã¾ã§ããã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã«ããã¦å²ãå½ã¦ãããå²å½ã¦ä½ç½®ã«ã¹ã©ã¤ããããããã¯ãä¾ãã°ã¬ã¼ã«ãè¦ã£ã¦ãããã¬ã¹ãï¼ï¼ã®ä¸ã®ã¹ãã¼ã¹ã®å¨å²ã«æ²¿ã£ã¦çµã¿ç«ã¦ãããããããªã¼ãæ¡åãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦éæããå¾ããããããªã¼ãåãã®ãé²ãããã«ãåè¿°ã®ç¹å¾´ï¼åºå®å·ã¯ãããããªã¼ãå®ä½ç½®ã«ä¿æãããã¨ãã§ãããããã¯ãï¼é¨åçã«ï¼ããããªã¼ãå²ãããããªã¼ã®ç«¯é¨ã®ãã©ã¹ããã¯ã·ã§ã«ï¼ã®æãåæ¹ã®ä½ç½®ã«åºå®å·ãéç½®ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦éæããå¾ãããã®é åã¯ããããªã¼ãéç½®ããå¾ã«ã¯å±ãã«ããã®ã§ãåºå®å·ã¯ãä¾ãã°ãã«ããéç½®ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦ä½åãªé¨åãå¿è¦ã¨ããã«åããå¶éãããããã«è¨­è¨ãããã¨ãã§ããããã®æ©è½ãéæããããã«è¨­è¨ãããå¯è½ãªå®æ½å½¢æã¯ãï¼å°ãªãã¨ãé¨åçã«ï¼ããããªã¼ã¢ã»ã³ããªãå²ã¿ãããã¦ç· ãä»ãã¾ãã¯ã¯ãªãã¯ãããã¨ãã§ãããããããªã¼ã®ä»ã®ç«¯é¨ã§ã¯ãåãã¯ãã«ããéç½®ãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦å¶éãããã¨ãã§ããããã¯ãã®é åããããããªã¼ãåãä»ãããã¦ããã·ã¼ãã®ä¸ã®åè¿°ã®éå£é¨ããå±ããããããã§ãããæå¾ã«ãããããªã¼ã¨ä»ã®é»å­æ©å¨ã¨ã®éã®é»æ°çæ¥ç¶ãè¡ããã¨ãã§ããããã¯ããããªã¼ã¢ã»ã³ããªããã®é»æ°ã¨ãã«ã of the battery into theplastic shell2 can be accomplished as follows. The battery is placed in the vehicle's internal space through an opening under the seat and a buddy space is installed in a later assembly step. The battery slides into the assigned allocation position in theplastic shell2 until it is housed in the foremost possible position available for battery assembly. This can be achieved, for example, by covering the rails and guiding the assembled battery along the perimeter of the space under thefootrest22. To prevent the battery from moving, the features / fixtures described above can hold the battery in place. This can be achieved by placing the fixture in the foremost position of theplastic shell2 at the end of the battery that (partially) surrounds the battery. Since this area is difficult to reach after placing the battery, the fixture can be designed so that movement is restricted without the need for extra parts, for example by placing bolts. A possible embodiment designed to achieve this function encloses (at least in part) the battery assembly and can be tightened or clicked. At the other end of the battery, movement can be restricted by placing bolts, as this area is easily reachable through the aforementioned opening under the seat to which the battery is mounted. Finally, an electrical connection can be made between the battery and other electronic devices, which requires electrical energy from the battery Safety Vehicles can be equipped with systems that monitor the vehicle to improve the safety of the driver, passengers if present, and bystanders (s). The active driver safety system has detected that the throttle requested by the driver exceeds the vehicle's possible performance or that it can safely handle the driver, passengers, or bystanders (s). When the throttle response can be actively controlled. The system collects data from various sensors and cameras in the vehicle and information about the environment from the internet and GPS. For certain decisions, data from sensors or the Internet is sufficient. Using all the information collected, the system then uses motor torque output, throttle response, motor speed, speed, maximum current drawn from the energy storage system, distribution, maximum braking power, anti-blocking system parameters or braking, etc. Limits or adapts any scooter characteristics such as braking characteristics, vehicle dynamics, adjustment of such suspension parameters (rigidity, damping coefficient), and the safety of nearby people as well as the driver and in some cases passengers. Can be secured.å®å¨ã·ã¹ãã ãä½ç¨ããããã®æå ±ãæä¾ãããµãã·ã¹ãã ã«ã¯ãããã¤ãã®ã¿ã¤ããå­å¨ãããï¼ã¤ç®ã¯ãè»ä¸¡ç¶ææ¨å®ãµãã·ã¹ãã ã§ããããã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãä¾ãã°ã­ãã¯ã¹ã¿ã³ãã«éæ­¢ãã¦ãããç´é²éè»¢ãããã¯ã³ã¼ããªã³ã°ãã¦ãããã¾ãã¯åé»ãã¦ãããªã©ãè»ä¸¡ãã¨ãå¾ãæ§ããªç¶æãæ¸¬å®ããã³è¨ç®ãããã¨ãã§ããæ¬¡ãã§å¯¾å¿ããåãéåº¦ãæ¶è²»é»åãªã©ãæ¨å®ãããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãéè»¢èããã³åä¹èä½ç½®ãµãã·ã¹ãã ã§ãããããã¯ãéè»¢èããã³ä»»æã®åä¹èãã©ãã«ããã®ããããã³å½¼ããä½ããã¦ããã®ããä¾ãã°è»ä¸¡ã«åº§ã£ã¦ããããããã¬ã¹ãã«ç«ã£ã¦ãããå·¦ã¾ãã¯çã£ç´ããè¦ã¦ãããã¨ãæ¸¬å®ããã³è¨ç®ãããã¨ãã§ãããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãç°å¢æ¨å®ãµãã·ã¹ãã ã§ããããã®ç¬¬ï¼ã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãè»ä¸¡ãã©ãã«ä½ç½®ããã©ã®ãããªã¿ã¤ãã®æ°è±¡ããã³å¨è¾ºã«ããã®ããä¾ãã°ã¢ã¹ãã¡ã«ãã§ã¯é·é¨ã®ã¤ã¿ãªã¢ã®ã¢ã«ãã¹ããã¼ãã®ä¸ã§ï¼ï¼Â°ï¼£ã®å¤ã®æ¥å·®ãã®ä¸­ãã¾ãã¯å¤éã®åã£ãéè·¯ã®ä¸ã«ããã®ããæ¨å®ãããã¨ãã§ãããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãè¿æ¥ç©ä½èªè­ãµãã·ã¹ãã ã§ããããã®ã·ã¹ãã ã¯ãäººéããã³åç©ã®ãããªçãç©ãè»ãå»ºç©ãæ©ãå·ãè¡ç¯ãªã©ã®ãããªçãç©ä»¥å¤ã®ãã®ã§ããå¾ãè¿æ¥ç©ä½ãè­å¥ãããã¨ãã§ãããä¾ãã°èªè»¢è»ã«ä¹ã£ã¦ããäººãªã©ãç©ä½ã¿ã¤ããçµã¿åããããã¨ãã§ãããThere are several types of subsystems that provide information for the safety system to work. The first is a vehicle state estimation subsystem. This first system can measure and calculate various possible conditions of the vehicle, such as resting on a kickstand, driving straight or cornering, or charging, and then responds. Estimate power, speed, power consumption, etc. The second system is a driver and passenger position subsystem. It measures and calculates where the driver and any passengers are and what they are doing, for example sitting in a vehicle, standing on a footrest, looking left or straight. can do. The third system is an environmental estimation subsystem. This third system is where the vehicle is located, what type of weather and surroundings it is, for example in the Italian Alps of thunderstorms on asphalt, in the sunshine outside 35 Â° C on the beach, or at night. It can be estimated whether it is on a frozen road. The fourth system is a proximity object recognition subsystem. This system can identify nearby objects that can be non-living creatures such as humans and animals, cars, buildings, bridges, rivers, streetlights and the like. Object types can also be combined, for example, a person riding a bicycle.ãããã®ï¼ã¤ã®ãã¼ã¿ã¿ã¤ããåéããããã«ãè»ä¸¡ã¯ãè¨ç®ã®æ­£ç¢ºæ§ã¾ãã¯ç¢ºå®æ§ãé«ãããã¨ãã§ããç°ãªãã¿ã¤ãã®å¥åãä½¿ç¨ãããã¨ãã§ãããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã¿ã¤ãã®å¥åã¯ãè»ä¸¡ããã³ã¦ã¼ã¶ã®æ§ããªå¤ãæ¸¬å®ãããã¨ãã§ããã»ã³ãµã«ãã£ã¦åéãããããããã¯ä¾ãã°å éåº¦è¨ãã¸ã£ã¤ã­ãè»è¼ªéåº¦ãã¹ã­ããã«ä½ç½®ãã¹ãã¢ãªã³ã°è§ããã¬ã¼ã­å§åãã¿ã¤ã¤å§åããµã¹ãã³ã·ã§ã³èµ°è¡ãã¢ã¼ã¿è»¸ä½ç½®ãã·ã£ã³ããåé¨æ¸©åº¦ã»ã³ãµãã·ã¼ãããã³ãããã¬ã¹ãã®å§åã»ã³ãµãã­ãã¯ã¹ã¿ã³ãä½ç½®ãã¡ã¤ã³ã¹ã¿ã³ãä½ç½®ãåä¹èç¨ãããã¬ã¹ãã»ã³ãµã§ãããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã¿ã¤ãã®å¥åã¯ãååãã«ã¡ã©ãã©ã¤ãåãã«ã¡ã©ãå¾ãåãã«ã¡ã©ãè¿æ¥ã»ã³ãµï¼ã½ãã¼ãã¬ã¼ããè¶é³æ³¢ãç£æ°ãï¼©ï¼²ãªã©ï¼ãæ¹¿åº¦ã»ã³ãµãå¤é¨æ¸©åº¦ã»ã³ãµãåå¼·åº¦ã»ã³ãµãªã©ã®å¤åãã¿ã¤ãã®ã»ã³ãµã¾ãã¯ã«ã¡ã©ããåéããããç¬¬ï¼ã®ã¿ã¤ãã®å¥åã¯ãï¼§ï¼°ï¼³ãï¼ï¼§ãï¼ï¼§ãï¼·ï½ï¼¦ï½ãï¼®ï¼¦ï¼£ãï¼¢ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ãªã©ã®æ§ããªæ¥ç¶å¯è½æ§ãéãã¦åéãããå¤©æ°äºå ±ãäº¤éç¶æ³ããã³éè·¯å·¥äºãæ¥ä»ãæéãå ´æãä»ã®è»ä¸¡ã¨ã®éä¿¡ããã§ã¹ãã£ãã«ãéä¼ãã¾ãã¯ä»ã®ã¤ãã³ããªã©ã®ããç¹å®ã®é åã«å¤ãã®äººããéããã¢ã¯ãã£ããã£ãææ°ãã¥ã¼ã¹ã«é¢ããæå ±ãã¾ãã¯éè»¢æåãããã¯å®å¨æ§è©ä¾¡ãå¤æ´ããå¯è½æ§ã®ããä»»æã®ä»ã®ã¿ã¤ãã®æå ±ãè¦ã¤ãããã¨ãã§ãããTo collect these four data types, the vehicle can use different types of inputs that can increase the accuracy or certainty of the calculation. The first type of input is collected by sensors capable of measuring various values for the vehicle and the user. These are, for example, accelerometer, gyro, wheel speed, throttle position, steering angle, brake pressure, tire pressure, suspension running, motor shaft position, shunt, internal temperature sensor, seat and footrest pressure sensor, kickstand position, main stand position. , It is a footrest sensor for passengers. The second type of input is an outward type such as forward-facing camera, lidar-facing camera, backward-facing camera, proximity sensor (sona, radar, ultrasonic, magnetic, IR, etc.), humidity sensor, external temperature sensor, light intensity sensor, etc. Collected from sensors or cameras. The third type of input is collected through various connectivity possibilities such as GPS, 3G, 4G, WiFi, NFC, Bluetooth, etc. with weather forecasts, traffic conditions and road construction, dates, times, places, and other vehicles. Activities that attract a large number of people to a particular area, such as communications, festivals, rallies, or other events, information about the latest news, or any other type of information that may change driving behavior or safety ratings. can be equipped with the forward-lookingcamera130 of FIG. 1 for recognizing local precipitation (eg, rain, snow, sleet) that works in conjunction with the aforementioned internet connection system for the same purpose. In addition, the forward-lookingcamera130 can be used to recognize local road or driving surface conditions (eg, puddles, pits, sand). In addition, forward-looking cameras can be used to determine local (solar) light levels, objects, obstacles, people, other vehicles, and so on. The forward-lookingcamera130 can further record traffic conditions, such as accidents. For example, the camera operates when the sound captured by the microphone (s) 133 of the embodiment of FIG. 23 indicates the occurrence of an accident such as a loud and long car horn sound, a fierce tire, and a loud volume. Or the image from the camera may begin to be stored. This requires sound analysis of the sound captured using any available control, such as a microcontroller or the CPU of a user / driver owned mobile device. If it is suspected that an accident has occurred based on the captured sound, the image from the camera is stored on the scooter or transferred to a remote server. The stored or transferred images may be associated from a point in time before the accident to a point in time thereafter. As an alternative to sound analysis, the gyroscope indicates that the scooter has rotated or overturned, or any measured acceleration exceeds the threshold, or the GPS sensor has moved or is about to move the scooter. When indicated, the camera may be configured to operate to record images around the scooter, more specifically from the front of the scooter. Similarly, the signal from the camera itself can be analyzed. In addition, the analysis may target detection of vandalism and registration of perpetrators instead of traffic images. Similarly, the forward-looking camera may also be used for face recognition of the owner in front of the scooter, as in other parts of the disclosure, particularly the backward-lookingcamera129 described in FIGS. 19 and 23. Allows locking or unlocking, such as the electronic locks described elsewhere in the disclosure.ã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ï¼ã¯ãå³ï¼ï¼ã®éè»¢èã¾ãã¯å¾ãåãã«ã¡ã©ï¼ï¼ï¼ãè£åãã¦ãåè¿°ã®ååãã«ã¡ã©ã¨åãç®çã§å±æçãªéæ°´éããã³æ°è±¡ç¶æ³ãèªè­ãããã¨ãã§ãããåæ§ã«ãé¡èªè­ãå¾ãåãã«ã¡ã©ããã®ç»åãä½¿ç¨ãã¦ãã«ã¡ã©ï¼ï¼ï¼ããã®ç»åãå¦çããã³ã³ãã­ã¼ã©ãä½¿ç¨ãããã¨ã§ãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ã«ä¹ã£ã¦ããäººãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ãéè»¢ãããã¨ãè¨±å¯ããã¦ããããæ±ºå®ãããããã£ã¦çé£ãé²æ­¢ãããã¨ãã§ããããã«ã¯éè»¢èã®å¿ã®ç¶æãæ±ºå®ããéè»¢èã®å¿ã®ç¶æã«åºã¥ãã¦å®å¨ã¬ãã«ãé©åããããã¨ãã§ãããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ã«ä¹ã£ã¦ããäººãè¨±å¯ããã¦ããªãå ´åãããã¯çäººã§ããå¯è½æ§ããããç»åãä¿å­ãããã¨ã¯ãã³ã³ãã­ã¼ã©ã«ãã£ã¦æ±ºå®ãããç»åèªä½ã®åæï¼é¡èªè­ï¼ãã¸ã£ã¤ã­ã¹ã³ã¼ããï¼§ï¼°ï¼³ã»ã³ãµã¾ãã¯å éåº¦è¨ããã®ä¿¡å·ãªã©ã«ãã£ã¦èµ·åããå¾ããæ¬¡ã«æ­£å½ãªææèããã³ï¼ã¾ãã¯å½å±ã¯ãæ½å¨çã«ã¯ãµã¼ããä»ãã¦è­¦åããå¾ããåç»ã®å½¢æã®å¾ãåãã«ã¡ã©ããã®ç»åã¯ãã¤ãã³ããæ¤åºãããåã®æéãããã®å¾ã®ããæç¹ã¾ã§ä¿å­ãããã¨ãã§ããããããã¯ãï¼ã¤ã¾ãã¯è¤æ°ã®éæ­¢ç»åãä¿å­ãããã¨ãã§ãããã¦ã¼ã¶ï¼æ­£å½ãªææèã¯ãä¾ãã°çé£ã®å±éºæ§ãé«ãå±éºé åã«é§è»ããã¨ããªã©ãé§åã¢ã¼ã¿ã®é»æºãåããã¦ããã¨ãã§ããã®æ©è½ãä½åããããã¨ãã§ããããããã¯ããã®æ©è½ã¯ãä¾ãã°ã¸ãªãã§ã³ã¹ãªã©ã®çé£å±éºæ§ãé«ãé åã«é¢ããæå ±ãå«ãã¦ã§ããµã¤ãããã®æå ±ã«åºã¥ãã¦èªåçã«ä½åããã¦ããããThescooter1 can be equipped with the driver or backward-lookingcamera129 of FIG. 23 to recognize local precipitation and weather conditions for the same purposes as the forward-looking camera described above. Similarly, face recognition, using images from a backward-facing camera, and using a controller that processes images fromcamera129, determines if a person riding a scooter is allowed to drive the scooter. Therefore, theft can be prevented, and even the state of mind of the driver can be determined and the safety level can be adapted based on the state of mind of the driver. If the person on the scooter is not authorized, it could be a thief. Saving the image is determined by the controller and can be triggered by analysis of the image itself (face recognition), signals from a gyroscope, GPS sensor or accelerometer, and the like. Legitimate owners and / or authorities can then potentially be warned via the server. Images from a backward-looking camera in the form of moving images can be stored from the time before the event is detected to a point in time thereafter. Alternatively, one or more still images can be stored. The user / legitimate owner may activate this function even when the drive motor is turned off, for example when parking in a high risk area of theft. controller may be connected to thedisplay174 and configured to visualize the display of scooter characteristics adapted by the controller on thedisplay174. For example, for scooter drivers, passengers and heavy cargo, the maximum speed can be reduced to slow the throttle response, and this adaptation of scooter characteristics can be visualized on a display, egdisplay174. The controller may be configured to attribute the safety score of the scale to a safety aspect determined by the sensor and adapt the scooter characteristics when the safety score exceeds a predetermined threshold. The controller may then be configured to fit a predetermined threshold for any safety aspect based on the safety score for another safety aspect. For example, the controller has determined traffic density detected using, for example, amicrophone133 indicating heavy traffic due to a high traffic noise input, or using a forward-lookingcamera130 or other available camera through image processing. The safety threshold for the safety aspect of speed can be adapted based on. The overall safety level is preferably determined by the strictest safety level of all individual sensors. For example, if the safety level based on vehicle speed is a safe value, but there is a lot of noise in the vicinity indicating heavy traffic in the vicinity, then the safety level is the noise detected by themicrophone133 or theforward camera130. Calculated based on the level, and the overall safety level is the more stringent traffic volume detected by themicrophone133 orcamera130. It is configured to determine. In that case, the safety level can be a weighted average of all sensors. safety level can be determined by processing each sensor input individually, thereby calculating a score, which is a measure of vehicle and driver safety, for each of the many sensors. Thresholds can be used to determine the safety level of each sensor. The weight due to safety aspects is determined, for example, based on an analysis of the driver's behavior, pre-determined based on experiments and / or simulations, determined based on the driver's behavior, and / or adjusted by the driver. It can be at least one of a group consisting of possible possibilities. The behavior of the user or driver can be used to evaluate the backward camera 129 (which can also be used to evaluate the driver's state of mind and permission to drive the scooter), accelerometer, steeringangle sensor152, wheel speed sensor, gyro. Safety levels can be determined by evaluation using any number of scopes, motor torques, throttle controls, or other physical motion sensors, and the sensor data is processed to statistic overall motion intensity. Calculated by measuring physical characteristics, the number of sudden operations per unit time is counted to assess the safety level, and more sudden operations have a lower safety level than less sudden operations. Means that. Comprehensive safety level calculations are driving by measuring information about how safe the situation is (eg, the number of interactions with the vehicle) for both the overall safety level and / or the overall vehicle safety level of the individual sensors. It takes as input) how much the person is using the interface, no matter how many touches on the screen it does not work, strong acceleration / deceleration or braking operation, sudden operation), and the safety level threshold and accordingly. It can be performed as determined by a matching algorithm that adjusts the weight of each sensor. More specifically, if the safety level is entirely or partially determined by the speed of the vehicle, the safety level can be:Level 0 = Safe, stopped vehicle, motor off (vehicle in parking space)Level1 = Standby, stopped vehicle, motor on (red light state)Level2 = low speed, vehicle speed <5km / h,Level3 = medium speed, 5 â¤ speed â¤ 15 km / h,Level4 = high speed, speed> 15km / h, etc.éåº¦ã®å±¤ã¯è»ä¸¡ã¿ã¤ãã«ãã£ã¦å¤ããããã¾ãã¯å»¶é·ããããã¨ãããï¼ãªã¼ããã¤ã«ã¯ãé«ééè·¯ãªã©ã®ããã®ãããªãå±¤ãããï¼ãä¸è¨ã®éç¤ºã¯ãä¾ç¤ºçãã¤ééå®çã§ãããä»£æ¿ã®ã»ã³ãµãä»£æ¿ã®å®å¨ã¬ãã«ã®æ°ããã³ä»£æ¿ã®é¾å¤ã®çµãä½¿ç¨ãããã¨ã¯ããã¹ã¦æ¬éç¤ºã®ç¯å²åã§ãããThe speed layer may vary or be extended depending on the vehicle type (motorcycles have additional layers for highways, etc.). safety sensor may include at least a speed sensor from the group comprising a wheel speed sensor, a GNSS or GPS154 positioning sensor and an accelerometer or gyroscope 155, and the controller may include at least from the group including maximum speed, torque, acceleration and the like. It is configured to adapt one scooter characteristic. The safety sensor may include acamera sensor130 and the controller is configured to determine the safety aspect from the group including at least the traffic density and the rear or front or side traffic distance. The camera image can then be processed to determine the traffic volume around the vehicle and the distance to other traffic. Image processing then counts the number of vehicle-like shapes, person-like shapes, motorcycle-like shapes (and other shapes that appear in traffic), and the size of these shapes for distance evaluation. May include considering. By using the driver-orientedcamera129, it is possible to determine the driver's attention level. Tracking eye position and face direction to determine where the driver is looking, and if you are facing forward and not looking at the screen for too long, the safety level will be higher and vice versa. If you are looking around most of the time, or looking closely at the screen, your safety level is low. The safety sensor may include amicrophone133, in which case thecontroller120 of the scooter of FIG. 2 is configured to determine the safety aspect from the group including at least the traffic density. Microphone inputs can be analyzed and traffic levels and congestion conditions can be calculated by measuring the statistical characteristics of sound, the overall sound pressure level, and the sound pressure levels in various frequency bands. Additional or alternative, the number of horn sounds or strong verbal utterances can be used to calculate the overall traffic density score, then the score can be thresholded or used with a matching algorithm, if possible. For example, other sensor inputs such as vehicle speed are also used to convert to a safe scooter may further comprise a communication, application or entertainment display (174) for at least one visualization for the scooter's non-essential application interface, where the controller is thedisplay174 based on the determined safety aspects. It is configured to enable or disable the application of. An application intended for visualization on ascooter display174 must claim permission to be active at a particular safety level. This is a permit that allows you to be active at a particular level of safety in the first place. All apps are allowed to run at the minimum safety level, and the review process of whether to allow the app to run or display interface visualization is preferably all above the minimum level. Applies to safety levels. The concept is that the current safety level is communicated to the app, allowing or requiring the app to change the user interface depending on the safety level. Changes can be achieved in many ways. The method means, but not limited to, changes in the appearance of user interface elements, including position, size, visibility, color, opacity, and level of blinking. For example, at a safety level that indicates low safety, less features should be available (eg, the video should not be allowed to be viewed when the driver is not stopped), and the icon should be. It can be hidden and large in size, making it easier to control from the peripheral vision. Or conversely, at a safety level indicating high safety, features that are not used at other safety levels may be displayed. Moreover, at certain safety levels, only one dedicated app designed for high speed use can be run. For example, a driver can stop at a traffic light to read news, send a whatsapp message or watch a video, or check social media, but as soon as the scooter starts driving, The interface turns into a driving mode where all of this is impossible, forcing the driver to focus on safe driving (and navigation).ç°ãªãã¿ã¤ãã®ã»ã³ãµãã«ã¡ã©ãªã©ãä½¿ç¨ãã¦ãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ã®ææ§ããã³ï¼ã¾ãã¯ç¶æãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ã®è·éããã³ï¼ã¾ãã¯ä½ç¨ããåãç°å¢ã®ææ§ããã³ï¼ã¾ãã¯ç¶æãéè»¢èç¶æãä¾ãã°å¤§èããèãæ¹ãå®å¨é¢ãªã©ãç£è¦ã¾ãã¯æ±ºå®ãããã¨ãã§ããã³ã³ãã­ã¼ã©ã¯ãã¹ã­ããã«å¿ç­ãã¢ã¼ã¿ãã«ã¯ãã¢ã¼ã¿éåº¦ãéåº¦ãã¨ãã«ã®ã¼è²¯èµã·ã¹ãã ããå¼ãåºãããæå¤§é»æµãåéãæå¤§å¶åé»åãã¢ã³ããã­ãã­ã³ã°ã·ã¹ãã ãã©ã¡ã¼ã¿ã¾ãã¯å¶åãªã©ã®å¶åç¹æ§ãè»ä¸¡ãã¤ããã¯ã¹ããã®ãããªãµã¹ãã³ã·ã§ã³ãã©ã¡ã¼ã¿ï¼åæ§ããã³ãã³ã°ä¿æ°ï¼ã®èª¿æ´ãé©åããããã¨ãå«ãç¾¤ã®å°ãªãã¨ãï¼ã¤ã®ã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ç¹æ§ãé©åããããã¨ãå¯è½ã«ãªããããã«ãã£ã¦ãã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ã¨å±ã«éã°ããéè»¢èãåä¹èããã³ï¼ã¾ãã¯è²¨ç©ããªãã³ã«åè¦³èã®å®å¨æ§ãé«ãããå¾ããUsing different types of sensors, cameras, etc., the mode and / or condition of the scooter, the load and / or force acting on the scooter, the mode and / or condition of the environment, the driver's condition, such as boldness and thinking, safety aspects, etc. The controller can monitor or determine the throttle response, motor torque, motor speed, speed, maximum current drawn from the energy storage system, distribution, maximum braking power, anti-blocking system parameters or braking characteristics such as braking, vehicle. This may be wireless or may use some kind of power transfer cable, egcable121 with theplug122 of FIG. A common embodiment of such a cable is, for example, a separate cable that connects to a connector to the power supply at one end and to another connector to the vehicle at the other end. In this case, the cables must be supported separately and occupy cargo space and require multiple actions to operate. The second embodiment uses a cable fixed to the charging station. This reduces the need to support the cable, but limits the ability to charge in a particular location. Also, when using fixed cables, they are not easy to replace and are relatively delicate components that may be required within the useful life of the product. As a third option, an embodiment is proposed in which the charging cable is supported by the vehicle but occupies less cargo space and is already connected to the vehicle to reduce the connection operation to the vehicle. Ideally, it may be incorporated as a single cartridge that is easy to replace. Furthermore, since it is automatically pulled in, further convenience can be provided to the embodiment ideally consists of a spring-loaded cable reel, schematically represented by a spool or reel 123 in FIG. 2, such spool being placed in the vehicle body or in a cable compartment on the vehicle body. Can be done. Although ideally placed on the scooter body, it is not necessarily placed in an inconvenient location for cargo storage so as not to reduce cargo bearing capacity. This can result in poor access to the cable reel for rewinding the cable to the reel after charging, so the reel is preferably a spring to automatically pull the cable into the cable compartment after charging the battery. It's a gimmick. Cable ends appear somewhere behind the lid or around the vehicle under existing overhangs. Ideally, the pull-in point should be located low in the vehicle, near the center of the vehicle's footprint, to reduce the possibility of the vehicle tipping over due to the force exerted on the cable. Also, for stability, the cable may extend out of the scooter body during charging through a passage located at or near the center of the contact area of the scooter on the road surface or pavement, such contact area. Is defined by a triangle defined by wheels and an extended stand. However, an alternative or potentially additional consideration is that the cable end must extend from the scooter body through the aisle high enough to prevent the cable end or plug 122 from contacting the road surface during operation. It must be. The reel cable spring assembly is integrated into a single cartridge that is easy to replace but only needs to be connected once to the vehicle. One realization of such a aforementioned embodiment is a cable reel built into the bottom of the opening seat of a scooter vehicle, the cable end of which appears in front of the seat, but the cable or Other positioning of thespool123 may be possible as well. Even if the opening sheet is locked, it can be used to secure the cable by blocking access to the pull-in point when not in use. In addition, guide rollers can be added to allow easy pulling and pulling from multiple angles. solution that uses thearray131 of FIG. 23 of the speaker 36 of FIG. 12 to form the listeningsweet spot132 of FIGS. 24 and 25 around the listening position of the operator (scooter driver) to generate sound. Measures can be proposed. In a conventional single speaker, the sound is radiated in a spherical shape, and the area of the radiated sphere is 4Ï * r2, and the acoustic intensity is attenuated, which is quadrupled for every doubling of the distance. If the speakers are placed in a line array, or especially in two essentially horizontal speaker arrays, the sound propagates like a cylinder with a corresponding surface area increase of 2Ï * r * h, if properly configured. It can be produced and the linear acoustic intensity decreases with distance, resulting in lower power requirements for a particular acoustic intensity at a particular listening position of thesweet spot132. Thehorizontal speaker array131, which is opposite the center plane of the scooter due to interference and is even potentially symmetrical with respect to the center plane of the scooter, is a normal back that is useful for operators / drivers. Shows a high vertical pattern of. A concomitant advantage is that it is less disturbing to pedestrians and other traffic users. When a wide range of audio is desired, for example when the vehicle is stationary and there is a larger audience, this can still be achieved by introducing speaker-to-speaker actuation delays. When the exact listening position is measured, for example using themicrophone array133 of FIG. 23, listening to the audio delay or listening from the head tracking camera, the listeningsweet spot132 is measured using the accurate speaker delay. You can focus more on the position. When the speaker array is attached to a turning body, such as the steering of a two-wheeled vehicle, the displayed pattern turns with the body. ã§ãããVoice recording may also be possible to make a call or record a memory message using themicrophone133 to register the sound. Voice recording is becoming increasingly important in vehicles due to the increasing integration of smart technologies that rely on voice input. In the case of open vehicles, there is no enclosure for the driver to sit down, so there is a major challenge due to the large amount of ambient noise associated with such vehicles. A solution to this consideration could be to use thearray133 of microphones in the processing of recordings to allow filtering of ambient noise such as wind and road noise while driving. This filtering can be done more accurately if more information about unwanted noise is known. Other vehicle sensors can be examined for this purpose. One of the main causes of unwanted noise is running wind. The effect of running wind on voice recording is highly dependent on vehicle speed and the main approach angle of the wind. Vehicle speed can be estimated from existing on-board sensors such as wheel speed sensors orGPS sensors154. The approach angle can be affected by static wind direction. The effect of this can be determined by assessing different sound pressure levels recorded by different microphones. The presence of large prevailing winds that are not completely tangential or perpendicular to the vehicle's trajectory will result in differences in the measured sound pressure levels. If properly calibrated, the wind direction and velocity can be estimated and used as an input for the calculated vehicle velocity and / or range.ãã³ã­ãã¯ã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼ã¯ãä¾ãã°ãã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ãã¹ã©ã¤ãã¾ãã¯ã¹ã¤ãã«ã®å½¢æã®åãè¾¼ã¿åã­ãã¯æ©æ§ãåãããããã¯ãéããç¶æã®å³ï¼ï¼ï¼¡ããã³ã­ãã¯ãããç¶æã®å³ï¼ï¼ï¼¢ã«æ¦ç¥çã«è¡¨ããã¦ããããã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãç¹å®ã®ææãä¾ãã°ç¡¬åé¼è£½ã§ãããç ´æ­ãããæããããã«ãããæ©æ§ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãä¾ãã°ã°ã­ã«ãã£ã¦ããã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ãã¹ã¤ã³ã°ã¢ã¼ã ï¼ï¼ã®éå¸¸å¼ãè¾¼ã¿ä½ç½®ã«ä¿æããããä¾ãã°ãã£ã¹ã¯ãã¬ã¼ã­ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¨ä¿åãããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦åè¨è»ä¸¡ã®ãã©ã¤ããã¬ã¤ã³ããã­ãã¯ããããã«å³ï¼ï¼ï¼¢ã«ç¤ºãä½ç½®ã«çªåºããããã¨ãã§ãããå¾èã¯ãåè¨ãã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ãã¹ã©ã¤ãã¾ãã¯ã¹ã¤ãã«ããä¾ãã°å¶åãã£ã¹ã¯ããªã ã¾ãã¯ã·ã£ããã®åå´ã®ã¹ã­ããã«çªåºããããã¨ã«ãã£ã¦éæããå¾ãããã®æ©æ§ã¯ãä¾ãã°ã½ã¬ãã¤ãã®ãããªé»æ°æ©æ¢°å¼ã¢ã¯ãã¥ã¨ã¼ã¿ã«ãã£ã¦ä½åããããã¨ãã§ãããé»æ°æ©æ¢°å¼ã¢ã¯ãã¥ã¨ã¼ã¿ã¯ãï¼£ï¼¡ï¼®ã¾ãã¯ï¼¬ï¼©ï¼®ãã¹ãªã©ã®éä¿¡ãã¹ã«ãã£ã¦å¶å¾¡ããããããã«ãããä¾ãã°ï¼·ï½ï¼¦ï½ãã»ã«ã©æ¥ç¶ãï¼¢ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ãä»ãã¦ãã¾ãã¯å±æç®çããã³é éã®ã­ãã¯ããã³ã­ãã¯è§£é¤å¶å¾¡ãå¿è¦ã¨ããä»ã®ãµã¼ãã¹ã«åè¨è»ä¸¡ãé©ãããã®ã«ããä»ã®ææ®µã«ãã£ã¦ãã­ãã¯ãé éã§å¶å¾¡ãããã¨ãå¯è½ã«ãªããThe pinlock swing arm62 comprises an embedded locking mechanism in the form of, for example, apin126, a slider or a swivel. This is schematically shown in FIG. 16A in the open state and FIG. 16B in the locked state. Thepin126 is made of a particular material, such as hardened steel, and is resistant to breakage and breakage. Themechanism127 holds thepin126 in the normal retracted position of theswing arm62, for example by a spring, but projects to the position shown in FIG. 16B to block the vehicle drivetrain, for example by engaging with thedisc brake128. Can be made to. The latter can be achieved by projecting thepin125, slider or swivel, for example, into a slot inside a braking disc, rim or shaft. This mechanism can be actuated by an electromechanical actuator such as a solenoid. The electromechanical actuator is controlled by a communication bus such as a CAN or LIN bus. This allows the lock to be remotely locked, for example via WiFi, cellular connectivity, Bluetooth, or by other means to make the vehicle suitable for other services requiring shared and remote lock and unlock controls. blocking of the drivetrain can cause potentially dangerous situations, so apply mechanical and electrical safety mechanisms to prevent thepin126 from being pushed out when driving a vehicle. Can be done. The safety mechanism can include (but is not limited to) one of the following solutions, or a combination thereof. The mechanism can be limited to actuating as the case may be, and the wheel speed sensor of thefront wheel80 does not measure the rotation of thefront wheel80 and is mechanically connected to the position sensor of the motor (rear wheel40). ) Does not measure the rotation of the rear wheels, the accelerometer can transmit a signal and deduct from the signal that the vehicle is stationary, and thepressure sensor26 measures the person sitting in thesaddle24. No, the motor does not transmit torque, and / or the rear brake is applied. In addition, the ends of thepin126, slider, swivel or spindle can have a particular shape, such as a hemispherical shape, which causes the pin to bounce off when it hits thedisc brake128, thus making the pin faster. Prevents you from entering the slot at wheel speed. In addition to this, certain mechanical safety mechanisms can be applied while the object is mechanically connected to the rear wheels and thus rotates at a speed similar to that of the rear wheels. This object can expand in certain ways as a result of the centrifugal force resulting from rotation. The expansion of the object prevents pins, sliders or swivels from entering and blocking thedisc brake128 of the drivetrain or any other drivetrain component while driving.åè¿°ã®ããã«ãã­ãã¯ã¯ãé éã§å¶å¾¡ãããã¨ãã§ãããã­ãã¯ã¨ã­ãã¯è§£é¤ã®ä¸¡æ¹ããé ãããå¯è½ã§ãããè»ä¸¡ãé éã§ã­ãã¯ãããã¨ã¯ããã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ãä¾ãã°ãã£ã¹ã¯ãã¬ã¼ã­ï¼ï¼ï¼ã®ã¹ã­ããã«å¥ãããã«å¾è¼ªãæ­£ããä½ç½®ã«ãããã¨ãå¿è¦ã¨ããã®ã§ãèª²é¡ãããããå¯è½æ§ããããä½ç½®ã»ã³ãµãåè¨ã¢ã¼ã¿ã«åãè¾¼ã¾ããåè¨ã¢ã¼ã¿ãå¾è¼ªã«æ©æ¢°çã«æ¥ç¶ãããã®ã§ããã®ä½ç½®ã»ã³ãµãå«ãã¢ã¼ã¿ãä½¿ç¨ãã¦å¾è¼ªããã©ã¤ããã¬ã¤ã³ãã­ãã¯ããããã®æ­£ããä½ç½®ã«è¨­å®ãããã¨ãã§ãããå¾èã¯ãå¾è¼ªãå°é¢ã¨æ¥è§¦ãã¦ããªãã¨ããä¾ãã°è»ä¸¡ãä¸­å¤®ã¹ã¿ã³ãã«é§è»ããã¦ããã¨ãã ãã§ãªããè»ä¸¡ãä¸­å¤®ã¹ã¿ã³ãã«é§è»ããã¦ããªãã¨ããä¾ãã°ã¹ã­ããã®æ°ãååã§ãããã¹ã¯ã¼ã¿ããããã«åæ¹ã¾ãã¯å¾æ¹ã«å¼·å¶ãããã¨ãã§ããå ´åã«å¯è½ã§ãããAs mentioned above, the lock can be controlled remotely. Both locking and unlocking are possible from a distance. Remotely locking the vehicle can pose a challenge as thepin126 requires the rear wheels to be in the correct position, for example to enter the slot of thedisc brake128. Since the position sensor is embedded in the motor and the motor is mechanically connected to the rear wheels, the motor containing the position sensor can be used to set the rear wheels in the correct position to lock the drivetrain. can. The latter is not only when the rear wheels are not in contact with the ground, for example when the vehicle is parked on the central stand, but also when the vehicle is not parked on the central mentioned above, the motor is mechanically connected to the rear wheels, for example by a toothed belt. It may be desirable to calibrate the position of the drivetrain (including one or more slots) with respect to thepin126. Calibration can be performed by the vehicle itself in order to reduce the work required for the maintenance of the vehicle. Automatic calibration is achieved by gently pushing the pin until it touches the braking disc. The position of the pin can be an external sensor by measuring the magnetic field of the electromechanical actuator or by assessing the stiffness of the applied spring in combination with a known force that the actuator exerts on the spring. Measured by a sensor. Such a measurement results in a certain movement of the spring, and thus a known distance in which thepin126 extends. When thepin126 touches thedisc brake128, a small force continues to press the pin against the braking disc. At the same time, the motor begins to rotate slowly until the pin enters the slot. The sudden movement of the pin is detected by the distance sensor and its position is stored by the motor controller and / or the electrical control unit. The position of the pin relative to the slot (s) is fully known and can be stored for future reference if it is desired to lock the vehicle.ã±ã¼ãã«ã­ãã¯ãã¼ã¹ãã¬ã¼ãï¼ï¼ã¯ãå³ï¼ã«æ¦ç¥çã«è¡¨ãããããã«ãæ¥ç¶ããããã®ããç¹å®ã®ã­ãã¯ãã³ï¼ï¼ï¼ã®ããã®æ¥ç¶ç¹ï¼ï¼ï¼ãåãããã¨ãã§ãããThe cablelock base plate42 may include aconnection point124 for aparticular lock pin125 for connection, as schematically shown in FIG.ãã®ããã«ãã¦ãã±ã¼ãã«ã­ãã¯ã¯ãåè¨è»ä¸¡ã«æ¥ç¶ãããã¨ãã§ãããåè¨æ¥ç¶ç¹ï¼ï¼ï¼ã¯ãé ãããå¶å¾¡ãããã¨ãã§ããã­ãã¯æ©æ§ãå«ãããã®æ©æ§ã¯ãä¾ãã°ã½ã¬ãã¤ãã®ãããªé»æ°æ©æ¢°å¼ã¢ã¯ãã¥ã¨ã¼ã¿ã«ãã£ã¦ä½åããããã¨ãã§ãããé»æ°æ©æ¢°å¼ã¢ã¯ãã¥ã¨ã¼ã¿ã¯ãï¼£ï¼¡ï¼®ã¾ãã¯ï¼¬ï¼©ï¼®ãã¹ãªã©ã®éä¿¡ãã¹ã«ãã£ã¦å¶å¾¡ãããã¨ãã§ãããããã«ãããä¾ãã°ï¼·ï½ï¼¦ï½ãã»ã«ã©æ¥ç¶ãï¼¢ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ï½ãä»ãã¦ãã¾ãã¯å±æç®çããã³é éã®ã­ãã¯ããã³ã­ãã¯è§£é¤å¶å¾¡ãå¿è¦ã¨ããä»ã®ãµã¼ãã¹ã«åè¨è»ä¸¡ãé©ãããã®ã«ããä»ã®ææ®µã«ãã£ã¦ãã­ãã¯ãé éã§å¶å¾¡ãããã¨ãå¯è½ã«ãªããIn this way, the cable lock can be connected to the vehicle. Theconnection point124 includes a locking mechanism that can be controlled from a distance. This mechanism can be actuated by an electromechanical actuator such as a solenoid. This allows the lock to be remotely locked, for example via WiFi, cellular connectivity, Bluetooth, or by other means to make the vehicle suitable for other services requiring shared and remote lock and unlock controls.
